Also include rep_id as a fixed effect\n\nThen the rep fixed effects tell us which reps are doing better/worse after controlling for everything else.\n\nBut actually, for the purpose of identifying underperformers, I think a simpler approach works:\n\n1. rep_store['endcap_rate'] * 0.15 +\n    rep_store['checkout_rate'] * 0.10 +\n    rep_store['promo_stand_rate'] * 0.10 +\n    rep_store['pos_materials_rate'] * 0.10 +\n    rep_store['planogram_rate'] * = ['rep_id', 'worst_count']\n\nrep_efficiency = rep_avg_rank.merge(rep_worst_count, on='rep_id')\nrep_efficiency = rep_efficiency.merge(sales_rep[['rep_id', 'first_name', 'last_name', 'region']], on='rep_id')\nrep_efficiency = rep_efficiency.sort_values('avg_rank')\n\nprint(\"=== Reps ranked by execution quality (lower rank = better) ===\")\nprint(rep_efficiency.to_string(index=False))\n\n# << 'PYEOF'\nimport pandas as pd\nimport numpy as np\nfrom sklearn.ensemble import RandomForestRegressor, GradientBoostingRegressor\nfrom sklearn.preprocessing import LabelEncoder\nimport warnings\nwarnings.filterwarnings('ignore')\n\nprint(\"Loading data...\")\nsales_rep = pd.read_csv('/app/sales_rep_001.csv')\nstores = pd.read_csv('/app/store_001.csv')\nvisits = pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f'/app/store_visit_{i:03d}.csv') for i in range(1, 13)])\nshelf_audits = pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f'/app/shelf_audit_{i:03d}.csv') for i in range(1, 13)])\nsales = pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f'/app/sales_transaction_{i:03d}.csv') for i in range(1, 13)])\ntraffic = pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f'/app/store_traffic_{i:03d}.csv') for i in range(1, 13)])\ninventory = pd.concat([pd.read_csv(f'/app/inventory_status_{i:03d}.csv') for i in range(1, 13)])\n\n# ============================================\n# APPROACH: Rep \"sales per unit effort\" analysis\n# For each store, compute total sales and total rep effort\n# Then compute each rep's contribution\n# ============================================\n\n# Step 1: Total store revenue\nstore_revenue = sales.groupby('store_id')['revenue'].sum().reset_index()\nstore_revenue.columns = ['store_id', 'total_revenue']\n\n# Step 2: For each rep-store, compute effort metrics\nrep_store_effort = visits.groupby(['rep_id', 'store_id']).agg(\n    visit_count=('visit_id', 'count'),\n    total_duration=('duration_minutes', 'sum'),\n).reset_index()\n\n# Step 3: For each store, compute total effort from all reps\nstore_total_effort = rep_store_effort.groupby('store_id').agg(\n    total_visits=('visit_count', 'sum'),\n    total_duration=('total_duration', 'sum'),\n).reset_index()\n\nrep_store_effort = rep_store_effort.merge(store_total_effort, on='store_id')\nrep_store_effort['visit_share'] = rep_store_effort['visit_count'] / rep_store_effort['total_visits']\nrep_store_effort['duration_share'] = rep_store_effort['total_duration_x'] / rep_store_effort['total_duration_y']\n\n# Step 4: Attribute revenue based on visit share\nrep_store_effort = rep_store_effort.merge(store_revenue, on='store_id')\nrep_store_effort['attributed_revenue'] = rep_store_effort['visit_share'] * rep_store_effort['total_revenue']\n\n# Step 5: Efficiency = attributed revenue / effort\nrep_store_effort['revenue_per_visit'] = rep_store_effort['attributed_revenue'] / rep_store_effort['visit_count']\nrep_store_effort['revenue_per_minute'] = rep_store_effort['attributed_revenue'] / rep_store_effort['total_duration_x']\n\n# Step 6: For each store, rank reps by efficiency\nrep_store_effort['rv_rank'] = rep_store_effort.groupby('store_id')['revenue_per_visit'].rank(ascending=False)\nrep_store_effort['rm_rank'] = rep_store_effort.groupby('store_id')['revenue_per_minute'].rank(ascending=False)\n\n# Also add shelf quality rank\nvs = visits[['visit_id', 'store_id', 'rep_id']].merge(shelf_audits, on='visit_id')\nrep_store_shelf = vs.groupby(['rep_id', 'store_id']).agg(\n    avg_facings=('facings', 'mean'),\n    eye_level_pct=('shelf_level', lambda x: (x == 'eye_level').mean()),\n    endcap_rate=('endcap_display', 'mean'),\n    checkout_rate=('checkout_display', 'mean'),\n    promo_stand_rate=('promo_stand', 'mean'),\n    pos_materials_rate=('pos_materials', 'mean'),\n    planogram_rate=('planogram_compliance', 'mean'),\n).reset_index()\n\n# Compute shelf quality score\nfor store_id in rep_store_shelf['store_id'].unique():\n    mask = rep_store_shelf['store_id'] == store_id\n    for col in ['avg_facings', 'eye_level_pct', 'endcap_rate', 'checkout_rate', 'promo_stand_rate', 'pos_materials_rate', 'planogram_rate']:\n        max_val = rep_store_shelf.loc[mask, col].max()\n        if max_val > 0:\n            rep_store_shelf.loc[mask, col + '_norm'] = rep_store_shelf.loc[mask, col] / max_val\n        else:\n            rep_store_shelf.loc[mask, col + '_norm'] = 0\n\nnorm_cols = [c + '_norm' for c in ['avg_facings', 'eye_level_pct', 'endcap_rate', 'checkout_rate', 'promo_stand_rate', 'pos_materials_rate', 'planogram_rate']]\nrep_store_shelf['quality_score'] = rep_store_shelf[norm_cols].mean(axis=1)\n\nrep_store_shelf['quality_rank'] = rep_store_shelf.groupby('store_id')['quality_score'].rank(ascending=False)\n\n# Merge efficiency and quality\nrep_store_all = rep_store_effort.merge(rep_store_shelf[['rep_id', 'store_id', 'quality_score', 'quality_rank']], on=['rep_id', 'store_id'])\n\n# Composite rank across efficiency and quality\nrep_store_all['composite_eff_rank'] = rep_store_all[['rv_rank', 'rm_rank', 'quality_rank']].mean(axis=1)\n\n# Step 7: Aggregate per rep\nrep_agg = rep_store_all.groupby('rep_id').agg(\n    avg_rv_rank=('rv_rank', 'mean'),\n    avg_rm_rank=('rm_rank', 'mean'),\n    avg_quality_rank=('quality_rank', 'mean'),\n    avg_composite_eff_rank=('composite_eff_rank', 'mean'),\n    total_attributed_revenue=('attributed_revenue', 'sum'),\n    total_visits=('visit_count', 'sum'),\n    total_duration=('total_duration_x', 'sum'),\n    store_count=('store_id', 'nunique'),\n).reset_index()\n\n# Count times best and worst\nrep_store_all['is_best'] = (rep_store_all.groupby('store_id')['composite_eff_rank'].transform('min') == rep_store_all['composite_eff_rank']).astype(int)\nrep_store_all['is_worst'] = (rep_store_all.groupby('store_id')['composite_eff_rank'].transform('max') == rep_store_all['composite_eff_rank']).astype(int)\n\nrep_best_worst = rep_store_all.groupby('rep_id').agg(\n    best_count=('is_best', 'sum'),\n    worst_count=('is_worst', 'sum'),\n).reset_index()\n\nrep_agg = rep_agg.merge(rep_best_worst, on='rep_id')\nrep_agg = rep_agg.merge(sales_rep[['rep_id', 'first_name', 'last_name', 'region']], on='rep_id')\n\n# Sort by composite efficiency (higher rank = worse efficiency)\nrep_agg = rep_agg.sort_values('avg_composite_eff_rank', ascending=False)\n\nprint(\"=== Reps ranked by efficiency (highest avg rank = worst efficiency) ===\")\nprint(rep_agg[['rep_id', 'first_name', 'last_name', 'region', 'avg_composite_eff_rank', 'avg_rv_rank', 'avg_rm_rank', 'avg_quality_rank', 'worst_count', 'best_count']].to_string(index=False))\n\nprint(\"\\n=== UNDERPERFORMERS (Worst efficiency) ===\")\n# Z-score\nmean_rank = rep_agg['avg_composite_eff_rank'].mean()\nstd_rank = rep_agg['avg_composite_eff_rank'].std()\nrep_agg['z_score'] = (rep_agg['avg_composite_eff_rank'] - mean_rank) / std_rank\n\nunder = rep_agg[rep_agg['z_score'] > 1.5].sort_values('z_score', ascending=False)\nprint(under[['rep_id', 'first_name', 'last_name', 'region', 'avg_composite_eff_rank', 'z_score', 'worst_count', 'best_count']].to_string(index=False))\n\nprint(f\"\\nNumber of underperformers (z > 1.5): {len(under)}\")\nprint(f\"IDs: {sorted(under['rep_id'].tolist())}\")\n\n# Also z > 1.0\nunder2 = rep_agg[rep_agg['z_score'] > 1.0].sort_values('z_score', ascending=False)\nprint(f\"\\nNumber of underperformers (z > 1.0): {len(under2)}\")\nprint(f\"IDs: {sorted(under2['rep_id'].tolist())}\")\n\n# ============================================\n# BETTER APPROACH: Model monthly sales with store+time FE\n# ============================================\nprint(\"\\n\\n=== MONTHLY MODEL WITH STORE FIXED EFFECTS ===\")\n\n# Create month-level data\nsales['month'] = pd.to_datetime(sales['sales_date']).dt.month\nvisits['month'] = pd.to_datetime(visits['visit_start']).dt.month\n\n# Monthly sales per store\nmonthly_sales = sales.groupby(['store_id', 'month'])['revenue'].sum().reset_index()\n\n# Monthly rep metrics per store (average across reps visiting)\nmonthly_visits = visits.groupby(['store_id', 'month', 'rep_id']).agg(\n    vc=('visit_id', 'count'),\n    td=('duration_minutes', 'sum'),\n).reset_index()\n\n# Monthly shelf metrics per rep-store\nvs_monthly = visits[['visit_id', 'store_id', 'month', 'rep_id']].merge(shelf_audits, on='visit_id')\nmonthly_shelf = vs_monthly.groupby(['store_id', 'month', 'rep_id']).agg(\n    facings=('facings', 'mean'),\n    eye_level=('shelf_level', lambda x: (x == 'eye_level').mean()),\n    endcap=('endcap_display', 'mean'),\n    planogram=('planogram_compliance', 'mean'),\n).reset_index()\n\n# Merge\nmonthly_rep = monthly_visits.merge(monthly_shelf, on=['store_id', 'month', 'rep_id'], how='left')\nfor c in ['facings', 'eye_level', 'endcap', 'planogram']:\n    monthly_rep[c] = monthly_rep[c].fillna(0)\n\n# For each store-month, average rep metrics\nmonthly_store = monthly_rep.groupby(['store_id', 'month']).agg(\n    avg_vc=('vc', 'mean'),\n    avg_td=('td', 'mean'),\n    avg_facings=('facings', 'mean'),\n    avg_eye_level=('eye_level', 'mean'),\n    avg_endcap=('endcap', 'mean'),\n    avg_planogram=('planogram', 'mean'),\n).reset_index()\n\nmonthly_store = monthly_store.merge(monthly_sales, on=['store_id', 'month'])\n\n# Add store characteristics\nmonthly_store = monthly_store.merge(stores[['store_id', 'store_type', 'store_size_sqm', 'location', 'region']], on='store_id')\nmonthly_store = monthly_store.merge(traffic.groupby(['store_id', traffic['traffic_date'].dt.month])['customer_count'].sum().reset_index().rename(columns={'traffic_date': 'month', 'customer_count': 'monthly_traffic'}), on=['store_id', 'month'])\n\n# Encode\nle_t = LabelEncoder()\nle_l = LabelEncoder()\nle_r = LabelEncoder()\nmonthly_store['type_enc'] = le_t.fit_transform(monthly_store['store_type'])\nmonthly_store['loc_enc'] = le_l.fit_transform(monthly_store['location'])\nmonthly_store['region_enc'] = le_r.fit_transform(monthly_store['region'])\n\n# Model: monthly revenue ~ store FE (store_id + month) + rep metrics\n# Since we have store fixed effects, we control for all time-invariant store characteristics\n# The rep metrics show how changes in rep behavior affect sales\n\n# Use GradientBoosting with store_id + month as features\nmonthly_store['store_id_enc'] = LabelEncoder().fit_transform(monthly_store['store_id'])\n\nX_cols = ['store_id_enc', 'month', 'monthly_traffic', 'avg_vc', 'avg_td', 'avg_facings', 'avg_eye_level', 'avg_endcap', 'avg_planogram']\nX = monthly_store[X_cols].values\ny = monthly_store['revenue'].values\n\nrf3 = GradientBoostingRegressor(n_estimators=100, max_depth=5, random_state=42)\nrf3.fit(X, y)\n\nfi3 = pd.DataFrame({'feature': X_cols, 'importance': rf3.feature_importances_})\nfi3 = fi3.sort_values('importance', ascending=False)\nprint(\"\\nFeature importance (monthly model with store FE):\")\nprint(fi3)\n\nmonthly_store['pred'] = rf3.predict(X)\nmonthly_store['resid'] = monthly_store['revenue'] - monthly_store['pred']\n\n# Now, for each rep in each store-month, get the residual contribution\nmonthly_rep_with_resid = monthly_rep.merge(monthly_store[['store_id', 'month', 'resid']], on=['store_id', 'month'])\n\n# The residual is shared by all reps in a store-month\n# But we can look at: within each store-month, which reps have better/worse execution?\n# And compare that to the residual\n\n# For each rep, compute average residual of the store-months they visited\nrep_resid = monthly_rep_with_resid.groupby('rep_id')['resid'].mean().reset_index()\nrep_resid.columns = ['rep_id', 'avg_monthly_resid']\n\nrep_agg = rep_agg.merge(rep_resid, on='rep_id')\nrep_agg = rep_agg.sort_values('avg_composite_eff_rank', ascending=False)\n\nprint(\"\\n=== Efficiency vs residuals ===\")\nprint(rep_agg[['rep_id', 'first_name', 'last_name', 'region', 'avg_composite_eff_rank', 'z_score', 'avg_monthly_resid']].to_string(index=False))\n\nPYEOF","description":"Sales per effort efficiency analysis","timeout":600000},"output":"Loading data...\n=== Reps ranked by efficiency
